#NOTE!!! Only actual Reforms go in here, not Legacy. Legacy go into 00_government_reforms.txt
monarchy_mechanic = {
    monarchy = yes
    heir = yes
    queen = yes
    basic_reform = yes # = invisible/does not take up a slot
    is_eligible_for_hre_emperor = yes
    valid_for_nation_designer = no
    custom_attributes = {
        enables_aristocratic_idea_group = yes
    }
    modifiers = {
        nobles_influence_modifier = 0.05
    }
}

#Feudalism vs Autocracy:

feudalism_reform = {
    icon = "castle"
    allow_normal_conversion = yes
    legacy_equivalent = feudal_monarchy
    valid_for_nation_designer = yes
    nation_designer_cost = 0
    potential = {
        is_ToR_subject_type = no
    }
    modifiers = {
        vassal_income = 0.25
        nobles_influence_modifier = 0.05
        maratha_exclusive_influence_modifier = 0.05
        rajput_exclusive_influence_modifier = 0.05
    }
    custom_attributes = {
        buffed_strong_duchies = yes #+5% Loyalty
        vu_has_ToR_subjects = yes #New VU 1.37.* Don Stuff
    }
    ai = {
        factor = 0.5 #generic
    }
}

elective_monarchy_reform = {
    icon = "ballot_box"
    potential = {
        NOT = { tag = POL }
        is_subject = no
    }
    allow_normal_conversion = yes
    valid_for_nation_designer = yes
    nation_designer_cost = 10
    fixed_rank = 8
    modifiers = {
        max_absolutism = -40
        all_estate_influence_modifier = 0.1
    }
    custom_attributes = {
        has_ruler_election = yes
    }
    ai = {
        factor = 0.25
    }
}

plutocratic_reform = {
    icon = "asian_scripture"
    allow_normal_conversion = yes
    legacy_equivalent = despotic_monarchy
    potential = {
        NOT = {
            culture_group = filipino_i
            culture_group = nakh_daghestani
        }
        OR = {
            technology_group = indian
            technology_group = muslim
            technology_group = chinese
            technology_group = east_african
        }
    }
    nation_designer_trigger = {
        OR = {
            technology_group = indian
            technology_group = muslim
            technology_group = chinese
            technology_group = east_african
        }
    }
    valid_for_nation_designer = yes
    nation_designer_cost = 10
    modifiers = {
        merchants = 1
        nobles_influence_modifier = -0.05
        burghers_influence_modifier = 0.05
        vaisyas_influence_modifier = 0.05
    }
    custom_attributes = {
        enables_plutocratic_idea_group = yes
        enables_aristocratic_idea_group = no
    }
    boost_income = yes
    conditional = {
        allow = {
            has_dlc = "Leviathan"
        }
        allow_draft_transport_ships = yes
    }
    conditional = {
        allow = {
            has_dlc = "Res Publica"
            NOT = { has_dlc = "Mare Nostrum" }
        }
        can_use_trade_post = yes
    }
    conditional = {
        allow = {
            has_dlc = "Mare Nostrum"
            NOT = { has_dlc = "Res Publica" }
        }
        can_form_trade_league = yes
        trade_city_reform = trading_city
    }
    conditional = {
        allow = {
            has_dlc = "Res Publica"
            has_dlc = "Mare Nostrum"
        }
        can_use_trade_post = yes
        can_form_trade_league = yes
        trade_city_reform = trading_city
    }
    ai = {
        factor = 0.75 #generic
    }
}

    }
    nation_designer_cost = 0
    modifiers = {
        liberty_desire_from_subject_development = -0.15
        nobles_influence_modifier = 0.025
    }
    custom_attributes = {
        buffed_strong_duchies = yes #+5% Loyalty

        vu_has_ToR_crowns = yes
    }

        set_government_rank = 6
    }

        factor = 101
    }
}

    icon = "austrian_archduchy_reform"
    allow_normal_conversion = yes
    #legacy_equivalent = austrian_archduchy_legacy
    valid_for_nation_designer = yes
    #fixed_rank = 7
    potential = {
        tag = HAB
        have_had_reform = austrian_duchy_reform
        is_part_of_hre = yes #Added on suggestion of Prussia. - SF
    }
    nation_designer_cost = 0
    modifiers = {
        liberty_desire_from_subject_development = -0.30
        nobles_influence_modifier = 0.05
    }
    custom_attributes = {
        buffed_strong_duchies = yes #+5% Loyalty
        vu_has_ToR_subjects = yes
        vu_has_ToR_crowns = yes
    }
    government_abilities = {
        habsburg_glory
    }
    effect = {
        change_dip = 1
        set_government_rank = 7
    }
    removed_effect = {
        change_dip = -1
        set_government_rank = 6
    }
    ai = {
        factor = 101
    }
}

austrian_dual_monarchy = { #For the Union of Austria Hungary/Equivalent with previous ME habsburg_monarchy_reform. Also, put this reform in the AUH country tag. - SF
    icon = "austrian_dual_monarchy_reform"
    allow_normal_conversion = yes
    valid_for_nation_designer = yes
    nation_designer_cost = 100
    #fixed_rank = 8
    potential = { #added via script
        OR = {
            tag = HAB
            tag = AUH
        }
        have_had_reform = austrian_archduchy_reform
        is_part_of_hre = yes #Added on suggestion of Prussia. - SF
    }
    trigger = {
        OR = {
            AND = {
                OR = {
                    senior_union_with = BOH
                    owns = 266
                }
                OR = {
                    senior_union_with = HUN
                    owns = 153
                }
            }
            tag = AUH
            has_reform = austrian_dual_monarchy
        }
    }
    nation_designer_trigger = {
        OR = {
            has_dlc = "Emperor"
            has_dlc = "Winds of Change"
        }
    }
    modifiers = {
        num_accepted_cultures = 2
        global_unrest = -2
        monarch_diplomatic_power = 2
        promote_culture_cost = -0.33
        tolerance_own = 1
        mil_advisor_cost = -0.15
        governing_capacity = 100
    }
    custom_attributes = {
        enables_religious_domination = yes #+1 tolerance of the true faith in catholic subjects
        vu_has_ToR_subjects = yes
        vu_has_ToR_crowns = yes
    }
    government_abilities = {
        habsburg_glory #Added in VU v1.37 by SF
    }
    effect = {
        change_dip = 2
        set_government_rank = 8
    }
    removed_effect = {
        change_dip = -2
        set_government_rank = 7
    }
    ai = {
        factor = 101
    }
}

austrian_absolute_monarchy = { #For the Austrian Empire/Equivalent with previous ME austrian_empire_reform. Also, put this reform in the AUH country tag -SF
    icon = "austrian_empire"
    allow_normal_conversion = yes
    valid_for_nation_designer = yes
    nation_designer_cost = 100
    #fixed_rank = 9
    potential = {
        OR = {
            tag = AUH
            tag = AUE
        }
        have_had_reform = austrian_dual_monarchy
        is_part_of_hre = no #Added on suggestion of Prussia. - SF
    }
    trigger = {
        OR = {
            AND = {
                absolutism = 50
                owns = 266
                owns = 153
                total_development = 500
            }
            has_reform = austrian_dual_monarchy
        }
    }
    nation_designer_trigger = {
        has_dlc = "Winds of Change"
    }
    modifiers = {
        num_accepted_cultures = 3
        culture_conversion_cost = -0.25
        culture_conversion_time = -0.2
        monarch_diplomatic_power = 2
        harsh_treatment_cost = -0.15
        monarch_diplomatic_power = 1
        governing_capacity = 150
    }
    custom_attributes = {
        enables_germanization = yes
        increase_nobles_loyalty_per_culture_conversion = yes
        vu_has_ToR_subjects = yes
        vu_has_ToR_crowns = yes
    }
    government_abilities = {
        habsburg_glory #Added in VU v1.37 by SF
    }
    effect = {
        change_dip = 3
        set_government_rank = 9
    }
    removed_effect = {
        change_dip = -3
        set_government_rank = 8
    }
    ai = {
        factor = 102
    }
}

    }

        }
    }

    modifiers = {

        }
    }
}

shogunate = {
    icon = "shogunate"
    allow_normal_conversion = yes
    potential = {
        NOT = { has_country_flag = formed_japan_flag }
        OR = {
            AND = {
                capital_scope = {
                    province_id = 1020
                }
                culture_group = japanese_g
                NOT = { exists = JAP }
            }
            AND = {
                is_playing_custom_nation = yes
                have_had_reform = shogunate
            }
        }
    }
    valid_for_nation_designer = yes
    nation_designer_cost = 50
    nation_designer_trigger = {
        culture_group = japanese_g
        technology_group = chinese
        capital_scope = { region = japan_region }
        owns = 1020
    }
    legacy_equivalent = shogunate_legacy
    fixed_rank = 8
    maintain_dynasty = yes
    allow_vassal_war = yes
    allow_vassal_alliance = yes
    lock_level_when_selected = yes
    can_change_primary_culture = no

    #Start of VU addition by San Felipe

    icon = "celestial_empire"
    allow_normal_conversion = no
    potential = {
        if = {
            limit = {
                has_dlc = "Mandate of Heaven"
            }
            is_emperor_of_china = yes
        }
        else = {
            OR = {
                has_reform = celestial_empire
                AND = {
                    culture_group = east_asian
                    num_of_cities = 50
                }
            }
        }
        NOT = { has_global_flag = empire_of_china_dismantled }
    }

    maintain_dynasty = yes
    allow_force_tributary = no

        culture_group = east_asian
        technology_group = chinese
        capital_scope = {
            OR = {
                region = north_china_region
                region = xinan_region
                region = south_china_region
            }
        }
    }
    factions = {
        temples
        enuchs
        bureaucrats
    }

    fixed_rank = 9
    start_territory_to_estates = 0.9

    modifiers = {
        prestige = 0.5
        church_influence_modifier = -0.1
        nobles_influence_modifier = -0.1
        burghers_influence_modifier = -0.1
        governing_capacity = 8000 #Increased to 8000 from 500 (EU vanilla) & Increased to 600 from 470 (GE) by San Felipe
    }

    ai = {
        factor = 1000 # should always be picked if available
    }

    custom_attributes = {
        locked_government_type = yes
        has_unify_china_cb = yes
    }

    conditional = {
        allow = { has_dlc = "Mandate of Heaven" }
        has_meritocracy = yes
        factions = {}
    }

kalmar_union = {
    icon = "kalmar_union"
    allow_normal_conversion = no
    potential = {
        has_dlc = "Lions of the North"
        has_reform = kalmar_union
    }
    trigger = {
        any_subject_country = {
            OR = {
                is_subject_of_type = danish_crown_PU
                is_subject_of_type = personal_union
            }
            capital_scope = { region = scandinavia_region }
        }
    }
    lock_level_when_selected = yes
    valid_for_nation_designer = no
    modifiers = {
        diplomatic_upkeep = 2
        advisor_pool = 1
        nobles_influence_modifier = 0.15
    }
    removed_effect = {
        hidden_effect = {
            if = {
                limit = {
                    NOT = { has_dlc = "Lions of the North" }
                }
                add_government_reform = feudalism_reform
            }
        }
    }

    custom_attributes = {
        locked_government_type = yes
        kalmar_union_succession = yes
        cannot_integrate_personal_unions = yes
        cannot_abandon_personal_unions = yes
        vu_has_ToR_subjects = yes
        vu_has_ToR_crowns = yes
    }
    ai = {
        factor = 1
    }
}

revolutionary_empire_reform = {
    lock_level_when_selected = yes
    icon = "rioting_burning_2"
    allow_normal_conversion = no
    potential = {
        has_reform = revolutionary_empire_reform
    }
    legacy_equivalent = revolutionary_empire
    valid_for_new_country = no
    uses_revolutionary_zeal = yes
    revolutionary = yes
    is_eligible_for_hre_emperor = no
    fixed_rank = 9
    modifiers = {
        global_manpower_modifier = 0.25
        land_morale = 0.10
        global_autonomy = -0.2
        governing_capacity = 2000 #No change in VU but was 150 GE
        max_revolutionary_zeal = 50
        papal_influence = -100
        allowed_rev_guard_fraction = 0.2
    }

    custom_attributes = {
        locked_government_type = yes
    }

    conditional = {
        allow = {
            has_dlc = "Rights of Man"
        }
        factions = {
            rr_jacobins
            rr_royalists
            rr_girondists
        }
    }
    removed_effect = {
        hidden_effect = {
            if = {
                limit = {
                    has_country_flag = is_revolutionary_china_flag
                    is_revolutionary = no
                }
                clr_country_flag = is_revolutionary_china_flag
                restore_country_name = yes
                override_country_name = CHINA_STRING
                set_country_flag = is_china_flag
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    has_country_flag = is_revolutionary_turkey_flag
                    is_revolutionary = no
                }
                clr_country_flag = is_revolutionary_turkey_flag
                restore_country_name = yes
                override_country_name = TURKEY_STRING
                set_country_flag = is_turkey_flag
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    has_country_flag = is_revolutionary_gurkani_flag
                    is_revolutionary = no
                }
                clr_country_flag = is_revolutionary_gurkani_flag
                restore_country_name = yes
                override_country_name = GURKANI_EMPIRE_STRING
                set_country_flag = is_gurkani_flag
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    has_country_flag = is_revolutionary_iran_flag
                    is_revolutionary = no
                }
                clr_country_flag = is_revolutionary_iran_flag
                restore_country_name = yes
                override_country_name = IRAN_STRING
                set_country_flag = is_iran_flag
            }
        }
    }
}

                name = msi_federal_kingdom_focus
                duration = -1
                desc = msi_federal_kingdom_focus_desc
            }
        }
    }

    removed_effect = {
        if = {
            limit = {
                has_country_flag = msi_unlocked_perma_reward
            }
            remove_country_modifier = msi_federal_kingdom_focus
            add_country_modifier = {
                name = msi_centralization_focus
                duration = -1
                desc = msi_centralization_focus_desc
            }
        }
    }

    conditional = {
        allow = {
            OR = {
                has_dlc = "Origins"
                has_dlc = "Cradle of Civilization"
            }
        }
        custom_attributes = {
            has_federal_kingdoms = yes
        }
    }

    conditional = {
        allow = {
            has_dlc = "Cradle of Civilization"
        }
        government_abilities = {
            tribal_federation_mechanic
        }
    }

    ai = {
        factor = 1
    }
}

                        id = flavor_gbr.20
                    }
                }

            limit = { has_country_flag = had_states_general_mechanic }

            have_had_reform = egyptian_government_reform

        }
    }

        religion_group = muslim
    }

        yearly_innovativeness = 0.1
        yearly_government_power = 0.5

    }

    government_abilities = {
        egyptian_westernization
    }
}

            is_lordship_subject_type = yes
            has_reform = eue_lordship_reform
        }
    }
    lock_level_when_selected = yes
    custom_attributes = {
        buffed_strong_duchies = yes #+5% Loyalty
    }
    modifiers = {

        cavalry_power = 0.15
        nobles_influence_modifier = 0.05
    }
}

unlocked_eue_lordship_reform = { #T1 - Lordship level
    icon = "eue_lordship_reform"
    potential = {
        has_reform = unlocked_eue_lordship_reform
        NOT = {
            is_lordship_subject_type = yes
            has_ToR_unique_government_reform = yes
            government_rank = 2
        }
        capital_scope = {
            superregion = europe_superregion
        }
    }
    #fixed_rank = 1 #Don't need this, as when you upgrade your govenment rank, you loose this one and gain the upgraded one
    custom_attributes = {
        buffed_strong_duchies = yes #+5% Loyalty
        vu_has_ToR_crowns = yes
        vu_has_ToR_subjects = yes
    }
    modifiers = {
        land_morale = 0.05
        cavalry_power = 0.15
        vassal_income = 0.05
        nobles_influence_modifier = 0.05
    }
    removed_effect = {
        if = {
            limit = {
                government_rank = 2
            }
            add_government_reform = unlocked_eue_barony_reform
        }
    }
}

            has_reform = english_monarchy

        }

unlocked_eue_kingdom_reform = { #T8 - Kingdom level
    icon = "eue_kingdom_reform"
    allow_normal_conversion = no
    valid_for_nation_designer = no
    potential = {
        has_reform = unlocked_eue_kingdom_reform
        NOT = {
            is_crown_subject_type = yes
            is_kingdom_subject_type = yes
            has_ToR_unique_government_reform = yes
            government_rank = 9
        }
        capital_scope = {
            superregion = europe_superregion
        }
        government_rank = 8
    }
    #fixed_rank = 8 #Don't need this, as when you upgrade your govenment rank, you loose this one and gain the upgraded one
    custom_attributes = {
        buffed_strong_duchies = yes #+5% Loyalty
        vu_has_ToR_crowns = yes
        vu_has_ToR_subjects = yes
    }
    modifiers = {
        land_morale = 0.05
        diplomatic_upkeep = 1
        monthly_splendor = 1
        tolerance_own = 1
        vassal_income = 0.35
        nobles_influence_modifier = 0.1
        nobles_loyalty_modifier = 0.125
    }
    removed_effect = {
        if = {
            limit = {
                government_rank = 9
            }
            add_government_reform = unlocked_eue_empire_reform 
        }
    }
}

#######################################
# TRANSITION FROM MONARCH TO REPUBLIC #
#######################################

#Step 11 - 01_government_reforms_monarchies (become a republic)
#Does not have legacy entry
become_french_second_republic_reform = { #become_rev_republic_reform
    icon = "second_republic"
    allow_normal_conversion = yes

    potential = {
        OR = {
            tag = FSR
            culture_group = french
        }
        is_revolutionary = no
        has_reform = first_french_empire_reform
    }

    trigger = {
        OR = {
            tag = FSR
            culture_group = french
        }
        has_reform = first_french_empire_reform
    }

    modifiers = {
    }
    effect = {
        if = {
            limit = { has_government_attribute = states_general_mechanic }
            set_country_flag = had_states_general_mechanic
        }
        set_country_flag = populists_in_government
        lose_reforms = 3
        change_government = republic
        add_government_reform = french_second_republic_reform
        if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = had_states_general_mechanic }
            country_event = { id = dutch_republic.33 }
            clr_country_flag = had_states_general_mechanic
        }
    }
    ai = {

#Step 15 - 01_government_reforms_monarchies (become a republic)
#Does not have legacy entry
become_french_third_republic_reform = { #become_rev_republic_reform
    icon = "third_republic"
    allow_normal_conversion = yes

    potential = {
        OR = {
            tag = TFR
            culture_group = french
        }
        is_revolutionary = no
        has_reform = second_french_empire_reform
    }

    trigger = {
        OR = {
            tag = TFR
            culture_group = french
        }
        has_reform = second_french_empire_reform
    }

    modifiers = {
    }
    effect = {
        if = {
            limit = { has_government_attribute = states_general_mechanic }
            set_country_flag = had_states_general_mechanic
        }
        set_country_flag = populists_in_government
        lose_reforms = 3
        change_government = republic
        add_government_reform = french_third_republic_reform
        if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = had_states_general_mechanic }
            country_event = { id = dutch_republic.33 }
            clr_country_flag = had_states_general_mechanic
        }
    }
    ai = {
        factor = 0
    }
}

#TIER 1 - ASSEMBLY
conf_parliamentary_reform = {
    icon = "judge"
    modifiers = {
        #tc_cities_influence = 0.25
    }
    trigger = {
        if = {
            limit = { NOT = { has_dlc = "Mandate of Heaven" } }
            NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
            NOT = { has_reform = revolutionary_republic_reform }
        }
    }
    conditional = {
        allow = { has_dlc = "Common Sense" }
        has_parliament = yes
    }
}
